 * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\\n245:      */\\n246:     @SuppressWarnings(\\\"fallthrough\\\")\\n247:     @Override\\n248:     public void authenticate() throws IOException {\\n249:         if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\\n250:             if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\\n251:                 return;\\n252: \\n504:     private boolean handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\\n505:         boolean isKafkaRequest = false;\\n506:         String clientMechanism = null;\\n507:         try {\\n508:             ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\\n509:             RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\\n510: (LOG.isDebugEnabled()) {\\n539:                     StringBuilder tokenBuilder = new StringBuilder();\\n540:                     for (byte b : requestBytes) {\\n541:
